<h1 class=3D"code-line" data-line-start=3D"0" data-line-end=3D"1"><a id=3D"=
EventDriven_and_PipesandFilters_System_0"></a>Event-Driven and Pipes-and-Fi=
lters System</h1>
<p class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"2" data-line-end=3D"3">This p=
roject demonstrates two architectures: event-driven using RabbitMQ and pipe=
s-and-filters using queues and processes. The system consists of several se=
rvices that process messages, filter them, convert them to uppercase, and s=
end emails.</p>
<h2 class=3D"code-line" data-line-start=3D"4" data-line-end=3D"5"><a id=3D"=
Project_Structure_4"></a>Project Structure</h2>
<ul>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"6" data-line-end=3D"10"><cod=
e>filters/</code>: Folder containing modules for each service in the pipes-=
and-filters architecture.
<ul>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"7" data-line-end=3D"8"><code=
>filter_service.py</code>: Service for filtering messages.</li>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"8" data-line-end=3D"9"><code=
>screaming_service.py</code>: Service for converting messages to uppercase.=
</li>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"9" data-line-end=3D"10"><cod=
e>publish_service.py</code>: Service for sending emails.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"10" data-line-end=3D"15"><co=
de>services/</code>: Folder containing modules for each service in the even=
t-driven architecture.
<ul>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"11" data-line-end=3D"12"><co=
de>api_service.py</code>: Flask API service to send messages to RabbitMQ.</=
li>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"12" data-line-end=3D"13"><co=
de>filter_service.py</code>: Service for filtering messages using RabbitMQ.=
</li>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"13" data-line-end=3D"14"><co=
de>screaming_service.py</code>: Service for converting messages to uppercas=
e using RabbitMQ.</li>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"14" data-line-end=3D"15"><co=
de>publish_service.py</code>: Service for sending emails using RabbitMQ.</l=
i>
</ul>
</li>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"15" data-line-end=3D"16"><co=
de>main.py</code>: Main file to run the pipes-and-filters system.</li>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"16" data-line-end=3D"17"><co=
de>rabbitmq.py</code>: Main file to run the event-driven system.</li>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"17" data-line-end=3D"19"><co=
de>README.md</code>: This file.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class=3D"code-line" data-line-start=3D"19" data-line-end=3D"20"><a id=
=3D"Installation_19"></a>Installation</h2>
<ol>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"21" data-line-end=3D"22"><st=
rong>Install Python</strong>: Ensure you have Python 3.6 or higher installe=
d.</li>
<li class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"22" data-line-end=3D"24"><st=
rong>Install Dependencies</strong>: Install the required dependencies using=
 pip.</li>
</ol>
<pre><code class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"25" data-line-end=3D"=
27">pip install -r requirements.txt
</code></pre>
<p class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"27" data-line-end=3D"28">Set =
up RubbitMQ</p>
<pre><code class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"29" data-line-end=3D"=
31">docker run <span class=3D"hljs-operator">-d</span> --hostname my-rabbit=
 --name some-rabbit -p <span class=3D"hljs-number">5672</span>:<span class=
=3D"hljs-number">5672</span> -p <span class=3D"hljs-number">15672</span>:<s=
pan class=3D"hljs-number">15672</span> rabbitmq:<span class=3D"hljs-number"=
>3</span>-management
</code></pre>
<p class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"31" data-line-end=3D"32">Run =
rabbitMQ services:</p>
<pre><code class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"33" data-line-end=3D"=
35">python rabbitmq.py
</code></pre>
<p class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"36" data-line-end=3D"37">Run =
pipes and filters services:</p>
<pre><code class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"38" data-line-end=3D"=
40">python pipes_and_filters.py
</code></pre>
<p class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"41" data-line-end=3D"42">To c=
ompare performance metrics, run this command</p>
<pre><code class=3D"has-line-data" data-line-start=3D"43" data-line-end=3D"=
45">python main.py
</code></pre>
